04020-
45˚ Brass 
Flare Fittings
•T wo piece construction – nut and body
• Use with copper, brass, aluminum, or steel tubing
•– 65° to +250° F. temperature range
• Standard fittings use short nuts. Long nuts are available for
higher vibration applications
• Resists mechanical pullout
• Easy to disassemble and can be reassembled many times,
with no effect on the seal
• Primary uses: fuel equipment, plumbing, gases, refrigeration,
and vacuum lines
To Assemble:
1 Cut smooth, square end on
tubing
2 Slide nut onto tube—
threads facing end
3 Flare end of tube
4 Thread nut to body 
until snug, then 
1/6th turn

Brass 
Inverted Flare
•T wo piece construction – nut and body
• Use with copper, brass, aluminum, or steel tubing
• –65° to +250° F. temperature range
• Seats and threads are recessed, protecting them
• Shorter overall length, for limited space applications
• Shorter nut allows tubing to be bent closer to fitting
• Fair vibration resistance
• Resists mechanical pullout
• Easy to disassemble, and can be reassembled many times, 
with no effect on the seal
• Primary uses: liquids, gases, and hydraulic brake systems
To Assemble:
1 Cut smooth, square end on
tubing
2 Slide nut on tube—threads
facing end
3 Flare end of tube
4 Thread nut onto body 
until snug, then 
1/6th turn
Tube O.D. 1/8 3/16 1/4 5/16 3/8 7/16 1/2 5/8 3/4

Anderson Metals Corporation, Inc.
15
Brass
Compression
Fittings 
• Three piece construction—nut, sleeve (or ferrule) and body
• Use with copper, aluminum, or plastic tubing 
(plastic requires 60P sleeve and 61P insert)
• –65° to +250° F. temperature range
• Standard fittings use short nuts. Long nuts are available for higher vibration 
applications. To buy compression fittings with long nut, please add a “1” in 
front of the part number. (i.e. 68 = 168)
• Easy to disassemble, no flaring tool required
• Primary uses: water, gasoline, oil, and vacuum lines
To Assemble:
1 Cut smooth, square end on tub-
ing
2 Slide nut, then sleeve onto tube.
Threads must face end
3 Insert tube into fitting
4 Thread nut onto fitting until
snug, then as follows:
up to 1/4″ 1 1/4 turns
5/16″ 1 3/4 turns
3/8″ and up 2 1/4 turns

00265-
Compression x
Compression
Computer Tube O.D. Weight Price
Number Size Per 100 Per 100
Brass 
Self-Aligning
Compression
Fittings
• Sleeve and nut permanently attached
• Sleeve is visible after installation, helping to eliminate misaligned sleeves
•T wo piece construction – nut and body
• Use with copper, brass, aluminum, or plastic tubing (plastic requires insert 61P)
• –65° to +250° F. temperature range
• Quicker assembly than flare or regular compression
• Better vibration resistance than regular compression fittings
• Can be used anywhere a regular compression fitting is used, especially when installation may be difficult
To Assemble:
1 Cut smooth, square end on
tubing
2 Slide nut over tube, threads
facing end
3 Insert tube into fitting
4 Thread nut onto fitting
until snug, then one more
turn

Poly-Connect®
Brass Flareless
Tube Fittings
• Three piece construction-nut, sleeve and body
• Use with copper, aluminum, plastic, or nylon tubing
(copper, aluminum, and nylon tubing requires
a brass sleeve)
• -65° to +250° F temperature range with brass sleeve
• -40° to +150° F temperature range with plastic sleeve
• POLY-CONNECT fittings do not cause twisting or weakening
of the tube, and can stand maximum movement of the tubes
• All fittings come pre-assembled with a fixed insert in the
body of the fitting which saves from 36% to 93% of the installation time
To Assemble:
1 Cut tube squarely and 
insert tubing into fitting
until it bottoms.
2 Then tighten only the nut
with the hands, no tools 
required.

Quik-Disconnect®
• Use with polyethylene, polypropylene, nylon & polyvinyl chloride tubing
• Quik-Disconnect® couplings with Poly-Connect® ends provide positive 
flow shut-off when coupling is disconnected, without extra valving. Available
in both single and double end shut-off
• For instrumentation and other applications where repeated connections
and disconnections are needed
•W ith a soft pressure of the thumb, the eyelet is disconnected from the
body of the fitting, closing the flow automatically at one or both ends
To Connect/
Disconnect:
Push - it’s connected. Unique
cam action automatically
moves the locking clip and
locks the coupling in an open
flow position when the two
sections are pushed together.
Flow is in either direction. 
To uncouple, press the 
locking clip and pull apart.
This action disconnects the
coupling and instantly seals
off the flow.CALL 1-800-821-5672    •    FAX 816-472-8700

Quik-Push®
Brass Push-In
Tube Fittings
• High quality all brass three piece construction with o’ring seal
• Use with plastic, nylon and soft metal tubing
• -40° to +200° F temperature range
•P re-applied Teflon® based pipe sealant on all conical 
male pipe threads, saves assembly time, as well as 
installation labor
• An interior hex combined with a 20% reduction in size 
over the original push-in design helps assembly in 
limited space applications
•A  new double bite collet for greater holding power
•A  37% increase in pullout performance over the 
original design
Quick Connect:
1 Cut tube end square.
2 Introduce tube into fitting
until it bottoms against the
internal tube stop, no tools
required.
3 Saves up to 75% of 
assembly time of standard
air compression fittings.
Quick Disconnect:
1 Press ring toward 
connection and pull tube
with the other hand, no
tools required.
2 In order to reuse tube, cut
its previously gripped end
and redo connection.

Anderson Metals Corporation, Inc.
34
Brass Fittings 
for Nylon Air
Brake Systems
• Three piece construction – nut, sleeve and body with attached insert
• Meets S.A.E. and D.O.T. specifications for nylon air brake systems
• –40° to +200° F. temperature range
• No special tools; flaring not necessary
• Excellent vibration resistance
• Used primarily in air brake and air accessory applications
To Assemble:
1 Cut smooth, square end on
tubing
2 Slide nut, then sleeve, onto
tube; threads must face
end
3 Insert tube into fitting
4 Thread nut onto fitting
until snug, then as
follows: for 1/4"
3 more turns

Quik-Dot® Brass Push-In
Tube Fittings
• High quality all brass three piece construction with eyelet and o’ring seal
• Meets D.O.T. FMVSS71.106 and SAE J1131 standards for air brake
system requirements
• -40° to +200° F temperature range
• Use with nylon tubing that complies with SAE J 844
•P re-applied Teflon® based pipe sealant on all conical male pipe threads, 
saves assembly time, as well as installation labor
•A  20% reduction in size over the original push-in design helps assembly 
in limited space applications and reduces weight
•A  new patented double bite collet for greater holding power provides 
a 37% increase in pullout performance over the original design
• Unique patented swivel design on elbows and tees provide full flow capabilities
• Captive eyelet with extended length is for easy assembly and allows 
for full flow. Top end radius eliminates scoring of tubing I.D.
Quick Connect:
1 Cut tube end square.
2 Introduce tube into fitting
until it bottoms against the
internal tube stop, no tools
required.
3 Saves up to 75% of 
assembly time of standard
air compression fittings.
Quick Disconnect:
1 Press ring toward 
connection and pull tube
with the other hand, no
tools required.
2 In order to reuse tube, cut
its previously gripped end
and redo connection.

for Copper Air
